# Sakuya Cheat Menu Pro - Block 3 Scripted GUIs

sakuya_main_force_show_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		is_player = yes
		has_variable = sakuya_main_force_show
	}
}

sakuya_main_force_show_clear = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		remove_variable = sakuya_main_force_show
	}
}

sakuya_main_03_01_mark_company_open = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }

	effect = {
		remove_variable = sakuya_main_force_show
		remove_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_use_marked_country
		remove_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_force_empty_notice
		trigger_event = { id = sakuya_main_03_01.1 popup = yes }
	}
}

sakuya_main_03_01_mark_company_open_marked_country = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }

	effect = {
		save_scope_as = sakuya_b3_root_country_scope
		remove_variable = sakuya_main_force_show
		remove_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_mark_country_found
		remove_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_use_marked_country
		remove_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_force_empty_notice
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target }
			scope:sakuya_b3_root_country_scope = { set_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_mark_country_found }
			save_scope_as = sakuya_main_03_01_marked_country_scope
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_mark_country_found
				exists = scope:sakuya_main_03_01_marked_country_scope
				scope:sakuya_main_03_01_marked_country_scope = {
					any_company = {
						NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_marked }
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_use_marked_country
			trigger_event = { id = sakuya_main_03_01.1 popup = yes }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_force_empty_notice
			trigger_event = { id = sakuya_main_03_01.1 popup = yes }
		}
		remove_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_mark_country_found
	}
}

sakuya_main_03_01_mark_company_clear_all = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	is_valid = {
		any_country = {
			any_company = {
				has_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_marked
			}
		}
	}

	effect = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				any_company = {
					has_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_marked
				}
			}
			every_company = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_marked
				}
				remove_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_marked
			}
		}
	}
}
 

# --- Trade & Market: 1. Trade Capacity ---
sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_active }
}

sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult } }
			set_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult add = 0.2 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_active
	}
}

sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_shift = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult } }
			set_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult add = 200 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_active
	}
}

sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_alt = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult } }
			set_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult add = 0.05 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_active
	}
}

sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_sub = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult } }
			set_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult add = -0.2 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult }
			add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult }
			set_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_active
		}
		if = {
			limit = { var:sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult = 0 }
			remove_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult
			remove_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_active
		}
	}
}

sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_clear = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity
		remove_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_mult
		remove_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_active
	}
}

# --- Trade & Market: 5. Ignore trade advantage penalty bool ---
sakuya_b3_tm_ignore_penalty_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { has_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_ignore_trade_advantage_penalty }
}

sakuya_b3_tm_ignore_penalty_add = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_ignore_trade_advantage_penalty }
	}
}

sakuya_b3_tm_ignore_penalty_clear = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_ignore_trade_advantage_penalty
	}
}

		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity_add multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_mult }

		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_mult } }
			set_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_mult value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_mult add = 100000 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity_add
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity_add multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_active
	}
}

sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_add_alt = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_mult } }
			set_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_mult value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_mult add = 10 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity_add
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity_add multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_active
	}

		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_mult add = -100 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity_add
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_mult }
			add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_trade_capacity_add multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_mult }
			set_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_active
		}
		if = {
			limit = { var:sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_mult = 0 }
			remove_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_mult
			remove_variable = sakuya_b3_tm_trade_capacity_add_active
		}
	}

# --- Trade & Market: 10. Disable trade centers ---
sakuya_b3_tm_disable_trade_center_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { has_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_disable_trade_center }
}

sakuya_b3_tm_disable_trade_center_add = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_disable_trade_center }
	}
}

sakuya_b3_tm_disable_trade_center_add_marked = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		is_player = yes
		any_country = { has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target }
	}
	effect = {
		clear_saved_scope = sakuya_b3_marked_country_scope
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target }
			save_scope_as = sakuya_b3_marked_country_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = { exists = scope:sakuya_b3_marked_country_scope }
			scope:sakuya_b3_marked_country_scope = {
				add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_disable_trade_center }
			}
		}
		clear_saved_scope = sakuya_b3_marked_country_scope
	}
}

sakuya_b3_tm_disable_trade_center_clear = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_disable_trade_center
		clear_saved_scope = sakuya_b3_marked_country_scope
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target }
			save_scope_as = sakuya_b3_marked_country_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = { exists = scope:sakuya_b3_marked_country_scope }
			scope:sakuya_b3_marked_country_scope = {
				remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_disable_trade_center
			}
		}
		clear_saved_scope = sakuya_b3_marked_country_scope
	}
}

# --- Company: 1. Max Companies (ported from BTN1) ---
sakuya_b3_max_companies_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { has_variable = sakuya_max_companies_active }
}

sakuya_b3_max_companies_add = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_max_companies_mult } }
			set_variable = { name = sakuya_max_companies_mult value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_max_companies_mult add = 1 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_max_companies
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_max_companies multiplier = var:sakuya_max_companies_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_max_companies_active
	}
}

sakuya_b3_max_companies_add_shift = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_max_companies_mult } }
			set_variable = { name = sakuya_max_companies_mult value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_max_companies_mult add = 10 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_max_companies
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_max_companies multiplier = var:sakuya_max_companies_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_max_companies_active
	}
}

sakuya_b3_max_companies_sub = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_max_companies_mult } }
			set_variable = { name = sakuya_max_companies_mult value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_max_companies_mult add = -1 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_max_companies
		if = { limit = {
				has_variable = sakuya_max_companies_mult
			}
			add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_max_companies multiplier = var:sakuya_max_companies_mult }
			set_variable = sakuya_max_companies_active
		}
		if = { limit = { var:sakuya_max_companies_mult = 0 }
			remove_variable = sakuya_max_companies_mult
			remove_variable = sakuya_max_companies_active
		}
	}
}

sakuya_b3_max_companies_clear = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_max_companies
		remove_variable = sakuya_max_companies_mult
		remove_variable = sakuya_max_companies_active
	}
}

# --- Company: 7. Create fixed company: company_united_tobacco_factories ---
sakuya_b3_company_create_random_enabled = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		is_player = yes
		NOT = { has_company = company_type:company_united_tobacco_factories }
	}
}

sakuya_b3_company_create_random = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		save_scope_as = sakuya_b3_root_country_scope
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_company = company_type:company_united_tobacco_factories }
			}
			add_company = company_type:company_united_tobacco_factories
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_company = company_type:company_united_tobacco_factories
				any_scope_state = { owner = scope:sakuya_b3_root_country_scope }
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = { owner = scope:sakuya_b3_root_country_scope }
				state_region = {
					save_scope_as = sakuya_b3_company_create_random_sr_scope
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { exists = scope:sakuya_b3_company_create_random_sr_scope }
				company:company_united_tobacco_factories = {
					set_company_state_region = scope:sakuya_b3_company_create_random_sr_scope
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

sakuya_b3_company_create_fixed_northern_thrace = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_company = company_type:company_united_tobacco_factories }
			}
			add_company = company_type:company_united_tobacco_factories
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_company = company_type:company_united_tobacco_factories
			}
			company:company_united_tobacco_factories = {
				set_company_state_region = s:STATE_NORTHERN_THRACE
			}
		}
	}
}

sakuya_b3_company_create_add_only = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_company = company_type:company_united_tobacco_factories }
			}
			add_company = company_type:company_united_tobacco_factories
		}
	}
}

sakuya_b3_company_recreate_fixed_northern_thrace = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_company = company_type:company_united_tobacco_factories
			}
			every_company = {
				limit = {
					type = company_type:company_united_tobacco_factories
				}
				owner ?= {
					remove_company = prev.type
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_company = company_type:company_united_tobacco_factories }
			}
			add_company = company_type:company_united_tobacco_factories
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_company = company_type:company_united_tobacco_factories
			}
			company:company_united_tobacco_factories = {
				set_company_state_region = s:STATE_NORTHERN_THRACE
			}
		}
	}
}

			limit = {

					has_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_marked
				}
			}
			every_company = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_marked

				}

	}

# --- Company: 11. Set marked character as executive ---
sakuya_b3_company_set_executive_enabled = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		is_player = yes
		any_country = {
			any_company = {
				has_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_marked
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			any_scope_character = {
				has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
			}
		}
	}
}

sakuya_b3_company_set_executive = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		save_scope_as = sakuya_b3_root_country_scope
		remove_variable = sakuya_b3_company_exec_company_ready
		remove_variable = sakuya_b3_company_exec_character_ready

		every_country = {
			limit = {
				any_company = {
					has_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_marked
				}
			}
			every_company = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = sakuya_main_03_01_marked
				}
				save_scope_as = sakuya_b3_company_exec_target_company
				scope:sakuya_b3_root_country_scope = { set_variable = sakuya_b3_company_exec_company_ready }
			}
		}

		every_country = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
				}
			}
			every_scope_character = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
				}
				save_scope_as = sakuya_b3_company_exec_target_character
				scope:sakuya_b3_root_country_scope = { set_variable = sakuya_b3_company_exec_character_ready }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = sakuya_b3_company_exec_company_ready
				has_variable = sakuya_b3_company_exec_character_ready
				exists = scope:sakuya_b3_company_exec_target_company
				exists = scope:sakuya_b3_company_exec_target_character
			}
			scope:sakuya_b3_company_exec_target_character = {
				set_character_as_executive = scope:sakuya_b3_company_exec_target_company
			}
		}

		remove_variable = sakuya_b3_company_exec_company_ready
		remove_variable = sakuya_b3_company_exec_character_ready
	}
}

# --- Goods: 1. Building goods input cost ---
sakuya_b3_goods_input_cost_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_cost_active }
}

sakuya_b3_goods_input_cost_add = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_cost_mult } }
			set_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_input_cost_mult value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_input_cost_mult add = -0.2 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_input_cost
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_input_cost multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_goods_input_cost_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_cost_active
	}
}

sakuya_b3_goods_input_cost_add_shift = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_cost_mult } }
			set_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_input_cost_mult value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_input_cost_mult add = -200 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_input_cost
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_input_cost multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_goods_input_cost_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_cost_active
	}

	scope = country
	is_shown = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_services }
}

sakuya_b3_select_good_services_toggle = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_services }
			remove_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_services
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_services
		}
	}
}

		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_opium }
			remove_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_opium
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_opium
		}
	}
}

sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_active }
}

sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_add = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult } }
			set_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult add = -0.2 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_construction_cost
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_construction_cost multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_active
	}
}

sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_add_shift = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult } }
			set_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult add = -200 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_construction_cost
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_construction_cost multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_active
	}
}

sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_add_alt = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult } }
			set_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult add = -0.05 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_construction_cost
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_construction_cost multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_active
	}
}

sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_sub = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult } }
			set_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult value = 0 }
		}
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult add = 0.2 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_construction_cost
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult }
			add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_construction_cost multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult }
			set_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_active
		}
		if = {
			limit = { var:sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult = 0 }
			remove_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult
			remove_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_active
		}
	}
}

sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_clear = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_construction_cost
		remove_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_mult
		remove_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_construction_cost_active
	}
}

sakuya_b3_goods_selected_input_mult_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		OR = {
			AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_ammunition has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_ammunition }
			AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_small_arms has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_small_arms }
			AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_artillery has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_artillery }
			AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_tanks has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_tanks }
			AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_oil has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_oil }
			AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_radios has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_radios }
		}
	}
}

sakuya_b3_goods_selected_input_mult_add = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_ammunition }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_ammunition } }
				set_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_ammunition value = 0 }
			}
			change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_ammunition add = -0.2 }
			remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_input_mult_ammunition
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { var:sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_ammunition = 0 } }
				add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_input_mult_ammunition multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_ammunition }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { var:sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_ammunition = 0 }
				remove_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_ammunition
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_small_arms }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_small_arms } }
				set_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_small_arms value = 0 }
			}
			change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_small_arms add = -0.2 }
			remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_input_mult_small_arms
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { var:sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_small_arms = 0 } }
				add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_input_mult_small_arms multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_small_arms }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { var:sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_small_arms = 0 }
				remove_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_small_arms
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_artillery }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_artillery } }
				set_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_artillery value = 0 }
			}
			change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_input_mult_artillery add = -0.2 }

sakuya_b3_goods_selected_output_mult_check = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = {
        OR = {
            AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_ammunition has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_output_mult_ammunition }
            AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_small_arms has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_output_mult_small_arms }
            AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_artillery has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_output_mult_artillery }
            AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_tanks has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_output_mult_tanks }
            AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_aeroplanes has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_output_mult_aeroplanes }
            AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_manowars has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_output_mult_manowars }
            AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_ironclads has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_output_mult_ironclads }

    scope = country
    is_shown = { is_player = yes }
    effect = {
        if = {
            limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_ammunition }
            if = {

            }
            change_variable = { name = sakuya_b3_goods_output_mult_ammunition add = -0.2 }
            remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_output_mult_ammunition
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { var:sakuya_b3_goods_output_mult_ammunition = 0 } }
                add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b3_goods_output_mult_ammunition multiplier = var:sakuya_b3_goods_output_mult_ammunition }
            }
            if = {
                limit = { var:sakuya_b3_goods_output_mult_ammunition = 0 }
                remove_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_output_mult_ammunition
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_small_arms }
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_goods_output_mult_small_arms } }

sakuya_b3_goods_selected_output_add_add = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = { is_player = yes }
    effect = {

sakuya_b3_goods_obsession_add_player = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = { is_player = yes }
    effect = {
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_ammunition } every_primary_culture = { add_cultural_obsession = ammunition } }
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_small_arms } every_primary_culture = { add_cultural_obsession = small_arms } }
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_artillery } every_primary_culture = { add_cultural_obsession = artillery } }

sakuya_b3_goods_obsession_add_marked = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = { is_player = yes }

        if = {
            limit = { exists = scope:sakuya_marked_country_scope }
            if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_ammunition } scope:sakuya_marked_country_scope = { every_primary_culture = { add_cultural_obsession = ammunition } } }

sakuya_b3_goods_taboo_add_marked = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = { is_player = yes }
    effect = {
        every_country = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target } save_scope_as = sakuya_marked_country_scope }
        if = {
            limit = { exists = scope:sakuya_marked_country_scope }
            if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_ammunition } scope:sakuya_marked_country_scope = { every_primary_culture = { add_cultural_taboo = ammunition } } }
            if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_small_arms } scope:sakuya_marked_country_scope = { every_primary_culture = { add_cultural_taboo = small_arms } } }

            if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_manowars } scope:sakuya_marked_country_scope = { every_primary_culture = { add_cultural_taboo = manowars } } }
            if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b3_sel_good_ironclads } scope:sakuya_marked_country_scope = { every_primary_culture = { add_cultural_taboo = ironclads } } }

sakuya_b3_has_marked_character_check = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = { is_player = yes has_variable = sakuya_b3_marked_character_cached }
}

sakuya_b3_sync_marked_character_cache = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = { is_player = yes }
    effect = {
        remove_variable = sakuya_b3_marked_character_cached
        if = {
            limit = {
                OR = {
                    any_country = {
                        any_scope_character = {
                            has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        }
                    }
                    any_character_in_exile_pool = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                    }
                }
            }
            set_variable = sakuya_b3_marked_character_cached
        }
    }
}

sakuya_b3_special_trait_ip4_check = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = {
        is_player = yes
        has_dlc_feature = ip4_content
    }
}

sakuya_b3_has_marked_character_and_country_check = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = {
        is_player = yes
        has_variable = sakuya_b3_marked_character_cached
        any_country = { has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target }
    }
}

sakuya_b3_can_set_selected_ig_leader_check = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = {
        is_player = yes
        has_variable = sakuya_b3_marked_character_cached
        calc_true_if = {
            amount = 1
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_armed_forces }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_devout }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_industrialists }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_intelligentsia }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_landowners }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_rural_folk }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_trade_unions }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

sakuya_b3_marked_character_commander_check = {

        is_player = yes

                has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target

sakuya_main_03_02_mark_character_open = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = { is_player = yes }
    effect = {
        remove_variable = sakuya_main_force_show
        remove_variable = sakuya_main_03_02_mark_country_found
        remove_variable = sakuya_main_03_02_force_empty_notice
        remove_variable = sakuya_main_03_02_page_2
        every_country = {
            limit = { has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target }
            root = { set_variable = sakuya_main_03_02_mark_country_found }
            save_scope_as = sakuya_main_03_02_marked_country_scope
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_variable = sakuya_main_03_02_mark_country_found
                exists = scope:sakuya_main_03_02_marked_country_scope
            }
            trigger_event = { id = sakuya_main_03_02.1 popup = yes }
        }
        else = {
            set_variable = sakuya_main_03_02_force_empty_notice
            trigger_event = { id = sakuya_main_03_02.1 popup = yes }
        }
        remove_variable = sakuya_main_03_02_mark_country_found
    }
}

# === B3 ROLE LIVE PATCH BEGIN ===
sakuya_b3r_has_marked_character_check = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = { is_player = yes has_variable = sakuya_b3_marked_character_cached }
}

sakuya_b3r_marked_character_commander_check = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = {
        is_player = yes
        OR = {
            any_country = {
                any_scope_character = {
                    has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                    OR = {
                        has_role = character_role_general
                        has_role = character_role_admiral
                    }
                }
            }
            any_character_in_exile_pool = {
                has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                OR = {
                    has_role = character_role_general
                    has_role = character_role_admiral
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

sakuya_b3r_marked_character_admiral_check = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = {
        is_player = yes
        OR = {
            any_country = {
                any_scope_character = {
                    has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                    has_role = character_role_admiral
                }
            }
            any_character_in_exile_pool = {
                has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                has_role = character_role_admiral
            }
        }
    }
}

sakuya_b3r_can_set_heir_check = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = {
        is_player = yes
        has_variable = sakuya_b3_marked_character_cached
        OR = {
            AND = {
                exists = ruler
                OR = {
                    has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
                    has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_theocracy
                }
            }
            any_country = {
                has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target
                exists = ruler
                OR = {
                    has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
                    has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_theocracy
                }
            }
            any_country = {
                exists = ruler
                OR = {
                    has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
                    has_law_or_variant = law_type:law_theocracy
                }
                any_scope_character = {
                    has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

sakuya_b3r_can_set_selected_ig_leader_check = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = {
        is_player = yes
        OR = {
            any_country = {
                any_scope_character = {
                    has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                }
            }
            any_character_in_exile_pool = {
                has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
            }
        }
        calc_true_if = {
            amount = 1
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions
        }
        OR = {
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = {
                            is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_armed_forces
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = {
                            is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_devout
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = {
                            is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_industrialists
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = {
                            is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_intelligentsia
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = {
                            is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_landowners
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = {
                            is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = {
                            is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_rural_folk
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            AND = {
                has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions
                any_country = {
                    any_scope_character = {
                        has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
                        interest_group = {
                            is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_trade_unions
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

sakuya_b3r_can_change_interest_group_check = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = {
        is_player = yes
        has_variable = sakuya_b3_marked_character_cached
        calc_true_if = {
            amount = 1
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk
            has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions
        }
    }
}

    scope = country

    effect = {
        sakuya_b3r_change_marked_character_interest_group_effect = yes
    }
}

        sakuya_b3r_set_marked_character_as_interest_group_leader_effect = yes
    }
}

sakuya_b3r_fx_transfer_player_agitator = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = { is_player = yes }
    effect = {
        sakuya_b3r_transfer_marked_character_to_player_effect = yes
        sakuya_b3_set_marked_character_role_effect = {
            ADD_ROLE = character_role_agitator
            REMOVE_ROLE = character_role_politician
        }
    }
}

sakuya_b6_reserved_build_infra_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		OR = {
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_reserved_build_infra_active
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_oil_rig
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_coal_mine
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_iron_mine
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_lead_mine
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_sulfur_mine
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_gold_mine
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_rubber_plantation
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_paper_mill
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_glassworks
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_tooling_workshop
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_steel_mill
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_motor_industry
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_power_plant
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_explosives_factory
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_arms_industry
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_artillery_foundry
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_munition_plant
			has_variable = sakuya_b6_build_sel_automotive_industry
		}
		OR = {
			any_scope_state = {
				has_decree = decree_sakuya_mark_state
				OR = {
					has_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b6_reserved_build_job_attractiveness
					has_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b6_reserved_build_job_attractiveness_default
					has_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b6_reserved_build_job_attractiveness_shift
					has_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b6_reserved_build_job_attractiveness_alt
					has_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b6_reserved_build_job_attractiveness_ctrl
				}
			}
			any_state = {
				has_variable = sakuya_mark_foreign_state_target
				owner = { has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target }
				OR = {
					has_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b6_reserved_build_job_attractiveness
					has_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b6_reserved_build_job_attractiveness_default
					has_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b6_reserved_build_job_attractiveness_shift
					has_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b6_reserved_build_job_attractiveness_alt
					has_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b6_reserved_build_job_attractiveness_ctrl
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
